## Arcs


## Anti-Patterns

- acting-out-emotions-as-fluidity Don't Confuse Acting Out Emotions with Emotional Fluidity (also: acting out emotions as fluidity, temper tantrums are not fluidity, yelling at people is not fluidity, crying at people is not fluidity, holding people hostage with emotion is not fluidity, out of control is not fluidity, the fluidity misreading, the I'm just being authentic excuse, the I'm in touch with my emotions defense, fluidity is not unloading, shame-driven emotion is not fluidity, the wild emoter misreading, the I let it all out trap, constricted emotion masquerading as fluidity, emotion as power move)
- coaching-as-savior-role Don't Coach to Save People (The Savior-Coach Pattern) (also: coaching as savior role, coaching from the savior role, don't coach to save people, the savior coach, the savior motivation for coaching, I want to save people coaching, saving people through coaching, savior childhood role becomes coaching, the rescuer coach, rescuer pattern in coaching, the emotional-caretaker-becomes-a-coach pattern, the alcoholic-parent child becomes a coach, I had to save my parent so now I save clients, coaching from rescuer, the savior dynamic in coaching, the comedian-to-coach version of the savior pattern, the kid-who-performed-becomes-a-coach pattern, the performer-to-helper transition, the still-trying-to-save-my-parents coach, saving parents through clients)
- coaching-as-surrogate-intimacy Don't Use Coaching as a Surrogate for Intimacy (Connection Without the Risk) (also: coaching as surrogate intimacy, coaching as a surrogate for intimacy, coaching as substitute intimacy, intimacy without risk through coaching, the coach who gets intimacy from clients, coaching as a substitute for partnership, the deep connection without the marriage risk, coaching to meet intimacy needs, surrogate intimacy in coaching, coaching as relationship substitute, intimacy that doesn't risk anything, the contained intimacy of coaching, I get my intimacy through my clients, coaching as one-sided intimacy)
- coaching-to-be-seen-as-wise Don't Coach to Be Seen as the One Who Knows (also: coaching to be seen as wise, coaching to be the wisdom holder, coaching to be the wise one, I want to be seen as the wise one, the wisdom-holder coach, the I-know-shit coach, the coach who needs to be seen as knowing, wanting to be the authority on, teaching to be the holder of wisdom, the I-have-the-answers motivation, I want them to come to me for the answers, wisdom-holder identity in coaching, the sage identity coach, the all-knowing coach)
- dont-add-anyway-to-love Don't Add 'Anyway' to 'I Love You' (Or 'It's Okay to' Before a Feeling) (also: don't say I love you anyway, the love-you-anyway trap, anyway as bypass, the anyway problem, I love you anyway makes the thing the bad guy, don't make the feeling the bad guy, the it's-okay-to-feel-X anti-pattern, the despite-X-I-love-you anti-pattern, the in-spite-of-your-pain-I-love-you anti-pattern, the love-you-despite-this trap, love around the thing instead of including it)
- dont-add-the-overwhelm-of-creating-the-overwhelm Don't Tell Someone They're Creating Their Overwhelm Before They Can See It (also: don't add the overwhelm of creating the overwhelm, you're creating your overwhelm as anti-pattern, premature responsibility for overwhelm, the responsibility-for-overwhelm trap, you can't be responsible for what you can't see, self-blame compounds overwhelm, the empowerment line lands as shame, right teaching wrong timing, the timing of responsibility)
- dont-believe-your-emotions-as-identity Don't Believe Your Emotions as Identity (The Emotional Fluidity Pitfall That Mirrors the Thought-Identification Trap) (also: don't believe your emotions as identity, don't identify with your emotions, emotions are not who you are, the emotion-as-identity pitfall, people start believing their emotions, the post-fluidity pitfall, the I-am-angry-not-anger-is-moving-through-me trap, rejecting thoughts and adopting emotions, emotions are good thoughts are bad is also a trap, the emotion-identification trap that mirrors thought-identification, emotional fluidity pitfall identification, the pendulum from thoughts to emotions)
- dont-block-emotion-waiting-for-reason Don't Block the Emotion While You Look for the Reason (also: wait until I know why before I feel it, demanding a reason for the emotion, blocking emotion until story is clear, I have to know why before I let myself cry, the reason-first trap, investigating emotion as suppression, why am I feeling this as block)
- dont-call-them-a-liar-with-deflection Don't Deflect Compliments (You're Calling Them a Liar) (also: don't call them a liar with deflection, deflecting a compliment is calling them a liar, you're telling them they're a liar, the polite-thank-you-while-still-thinking-they're-a-liar, deflecting compliments is rude, deflecting compliments costs them, the deflection-as-disagreement anti-pattern, deflection contradicts the giver, saying thank you while disbelieving is still deflection, the polite-deflection trap, the polite-disbelief deflection, the I'll-be-polite-but-disbelieve move, no I'm not the pretty one move, the you're-the-pretty-one deflection, deflecting hurts the giver, the compliment-giver felt rejection, the giver stops giving compliments after deflection, the deflection costs the relationship, the unreceived compliment as rejection of the giver, saying thank you is not enough you have to receive)
- dont-cement-insight-as-identity Don't Cement the Insight into a New Identity (also: don't cement the insight as identity, don't make the insight your identity, the insight as identity trap, don't make the aha a new self-image, insight as identity sabotage, defending the knowing, I already know this defense, the I-know-this-already trap, insight cemented into ego, using the insight to cement an identity, the insight becomes the new identity, claiming the insight as who I am, the insight as a new badge)
- dont-comfort-the-mourner-from-your-own-discomfort Don't Comfort the Mourner From Your Own Discomfort (The Funeral Pattern) (also: don't tell the mourner it'll be okay, the funeral pattern, comforting from your own discomfort, managing the mourner so you don't have to feel, are you okay as comfort, the are-you-okay funeral pattern, the say-something-to-make-them-feel-better pattern, the funeral comfort anti-pattern, fixing grief because you can't sit with grief, the obligation the mourner feels at their own funeral, don't make the mourner take care of you emotionally, discharging your own grief into the mourner's grief, the standard funeral failure mode, why funerals don't work, the bad funeral pattern, stop trying to make them feel better, feel-better-isms at funerals, the most-people-experience-of-a-funeral pattern, don't ask the mourner to perform okay-ness, loading obligation onto the mourner)
- dont-conflate-the-bliss-with-the-insight Don't Conflate the Bliss State With the Insight Itself (also: bliss leaving means insight is leaving, I had it and I lost it, mistaking the state for the recognition, the post-aha collapse, I lost the insight when the high faded, conflating ecstasy with insight, the insight didn't go away the state did, state-fade misread as insight-loss)
- dont-confuse-embracing-fear-with-inviting-danger Don't Confuse Embracing Fear With Inviting Danger (also: embracing fear is not creating fear, don't manufacture danger to practice fear, embracing fear doesn't mean reckless action, feeling fear isn't ignoring fear, the embrace-fear misreading, embracing fear vs being reckless)
- dont-defer-decisions-to-large-committees Don't Defer Decisions to Large Committees (also: committee decision making, deferring decisions to groups over 6, groups over 6 can't decide, committee dysfunction, decision-by-committee anti-pattern, more than 5 direct reports, over 8 direct reports red flag, committee decision trap)
- dont-dismiss-exercise-before-doing-it Don't Dismiss an Exercise as a 'Nothing Burger' Before Doing It (also: the nothing burger dismissal, we've done this before this isn't going to be useful, preemptive dismissal of exercises, this won't work for me as defense, the nothing burger defense, dismissing the exercise as cover, I already know what this will produce, we did something like this before, this seems pointless before trying it, the seems-too-simple dismissal)
- dont-do-anger-at-your-partner Don't Discharge Anger At Your Partner (Move It First, Then Talk) (also: don't yell at your partner, don't do anger at people, don't discharge at partner, yelling at partner anti-pattern, anger release is not anger at partner, move anger somewhere else first, don't aim anger at partner, the discharge-at-partner anti-pattern, release anger before the conversation, I'm just expressing my feelings as bypass, don't use the relationship as your gym for anger, don't make your partner take your anger work, the unconsented anger dump, don't yell at your partner to get the anger out, no permission no anger dump)
- dont-evangelize-the-work Don't evangelize the work (also: missionary work, using tools without permission, pushing transformation on others, coaching without consent, tools without shadow work, carrying someone else's tools without consciousness)
- dont-extract-apologies Don't Extract Apologies (From Kids, Partners, or Subordinates) (also: don't make people say sorry, don't force kids to apologize, stop extracting apologies, no extracted apology, extracting apologies installs shame, say you're sorry trap, the extracted apology anti-pattern, forcing an apology, demanding an apology, weaponized apology demand)
- dont-fight-identity Don't Fight Identity (or Ego) -- It Only Makes It Stick Harder (also: don't fight identity, don't fight your ego, killing the ego doesn't work, the egoless one is still an identity, fighting identity strengthens it, no boxing with the ego, Chinese finger trap for ego, ego deconstruction as identity, anti-identity is identity, the kill-your-ego trap)
- dont-fight-the-voice Don't Use the Voice to Silence the Voice (also: thief security guard, thief as security, fighting the voice, war with the voice, voice vs voice, attacking the inner critic, trying to silence the voice)
- dont-forget-the-tool-when-things-feel-good Don't Forget Emotional Inquiry Once Things Feel Good (The Relief-Period Drop) (also: don't forget the tool when things feel good, the relief period drop, abandoning the practice after relief, the everything-is-fine forgetting, the practice falls out of awareness after success, the post-relief forgetting, the one and done assumption about emotional work, I felt the sadness and it's done, transformation is not one and done, the practice needs revisiting)
- dont-go-after-every-emotion-at-once Don't Go After Every Emotion At Once (The Type A Pitfall) (also: don't go after every emotion at once, the Type A emotional inquiry pitfall, transformation too fast becomes ungroundedness, the type A pitfall in emotional work, embracing emotions as an in-it-to-win-it project, the self-reliant pitfall in emotional work, going after every emotion produces ungroundedness, the speed pitfall of emotional inquiry, don't push yourself to embrace faster, pushing to get there is another form of avoidance, take care of your nervous system during intensive emotional work, rest and massage and hot baths during intensive practice, the nervous system care prerequisite, no rush to emotional work, your pain will still be there)
- dont-half-ass-the-experiment Don't Half-Ass the Experiment (also: don't half ass the experiment, the unclean experiment problem, performing the practice without doing it, half-assing a practice, the false negative trap, going through the motions, the lazy gratitude problem, you can't learn from a dirty experiment, all-in or not-in, the half-hearted practice problem)
- dont-identify-as-awakened Don't Identify as Awakened (Or as Part of the Awakened-People Club) (also: don't identify as awakened, the awakened identity trap, I'm one of the awakened ones trap, putting yourself above others through awakening, the awakened-people club, the awakening identity, spiritual identification as superiority, I'm an awakened person identity, the people-who-had-the-experience club, subtle spiritual superiority, the awakening identity rut)
- dont-indulge-emotion-instead-of-welcoming Don't Indulge the Emotion Instead of Welcoming It (also: don't indulge the emotion, indulging vs welcoming, indulging uncomfortable emotions, feeling vs welcoming distinction, feeling shame without welcoming shame, feeling the emotion but not loving it, the indulge trap, wallowing in shame, wallowing in sadness, sitting in the emotion without welcoming it, feeling without curiosity, feeling without wonder, feeling without impartiality, the indulgence-without-welcoming trap, the in-between space between resistance and welcoming, feeling the emotion vs falling in love with the emotion, the indulgence problem, I'm feeling it why isn't it moving, I feel the shame but it won't go away)
- dont-jump-to-compassion-before-anger Don't Jump to Compassion Before the Anger Has Moved (also: compassion as bypass, the compassion jump, they had their reasons trap, reasonableness as suppression, premature compassion, compassion before anger, skipping anger with compassion, compassion order-of-operations problem, premature love, premature virtue, premature-virtue moves, premature love before heartbreak, skipping the descent through blockers with love, love as the premature answer, the right-answer-is-love trap, saying love as the answer, love as bypass when it's premature)
- dont-lean-into-conflict-from-defendedness Don't Lean Into Conflict From Defendedness (Or From 'I Won't Get What I Want') (also: don't lean into conflict from defendedness, leaning in defended creates conflict, armored leaning in, the fight-disguised-as-leaning-in, why did you do that as conflict creation, leaning in starts the fight, I'm not avoiding conflict as a defense, leaning in from the wrong place, leaning in while armored, leaning in while expecting to lose, the not-conflict-avoidant excuse for fighting, the defended lean-in, leaning in dressed as growth work)

## Principles

- a-support-system-creates-you You Create the Support System, the Support System Creates You (The Relief from I-I-I) (also: a support system creates you, you create your support system to be created by it, the support system creates you, I'm gonna create my support group only for my support group to create me, the I-I-I relief from support, stop carrying the whole thing alone, you're part of something greater, the gift of being created by the group, the humility-and-gratitude of being supported, I wouldn't be where I am without my support systems, you might be dead without yours, the I-have-to-do-it-all-myself relief, the relief of not doing it alone, let the group do what only the group can do, the support system as co-creator of your life, the not-it's-all-on-me relief, becoming a product of your environment by design)
- acceptance-as-change-strategy Acceptance Is the Most Effective Path to Change (also: accept then change, acceptance enables change, fighting is inefficient, accept how it is to change how it will be, acceptance is not resignation, love and accept and ask to change, acceptance vs resignation)
- acknowledging-death-compresses-life Acknowledging Death Compresses Life (Everything Becomes Sweeter, More Vibrant, More Meaningful) (also: death compresses life, acknowledging death compresses life, the closer to death the closer to life, everything is fleeting, coming coming going going, compressing life, the compression of life through death, viscerally acknowledging fleetingness, death makes life sweeter, the sweetness only the void gives, the sweetness that requires acknowledging emptiness, you don't get to taste the sweetness without acknowledging the void, the compression that mortality unlocks, the freedom of seeing through the illusion, compressed life from acknowledged death, fleetingness as the doorway, the abyss gives sweetness, the void you don't acknowledge keeps you from the sweetness, acknowledging mortality is life-affirming not morbid, Buddha's first words after awakening, the recognition that nothing survives this, the freedom of seeing nothing survives)
- acting-as-if-already-true Acting As If Your Vision Is Already True (also: live the vision now, be the change already, visionary action, as if reality, the world bends toward your truth)
- address-the-blocker-not-the-symptom Address What's In the Way, Not the Surface Problem (also: address the blocker not the symptom, address the obstacle not the goal, work on what gets in the way, the root cause approach, don't work on the symptom, the smoking and the starting a business have the same block, fixing the block changes ten things, work on the blockers)
- adversity-as-for-not-against Adversity Is For You, Not Against You (The Wheelbarrow Falls) (also: adversity is for you, God doesn't do things to us he does them for us, what you wanted would have hurt you, the protection in not getting what you wanted, thank God for unanswered prayers, the wheelbarrow falls and refines, loss as refinement, the painful protection, I was protected by not getting it, the disaster that becomes a gift, fragility of life brings gratitude, almost losing our life brings us closer to gratitude, confronting fragility produces gratitude)
